<script>
    
    function setcook() {
        var nazwa = 'cookie_tm';
        var wartosc = '1';
        var expire = new Date();
        expire.setMonth(expire.getMonth() + 12);
        document.cookie = nazwa + "=" + escape(wartosc) + ";path=/;" + ((expire == null) ? "" : ("; expires=" + expire.toGMTString()))
    }

    
        

    
        
        function closeTmNotify() {
                        $('#cookieNotice').animate(
                    {bottom: '-200px'},
                    2500, function () {
                        $('#cookieNotice').hide();
                    });
            setcook();
                    }
    
        
    
</script>
